FP-011 파일권한 Crontab 설정파일 권한 설정 적절성 FAIL /etc/at.allow.exists: False /etc/at.allow.group_gid: /etc/at.allow.mode: /etc/at.allow.mode_int: /etc/at.allow.others_write: /etc/at.allow.owner_uid: /etc/at.allow.path: /etc/at.allow /etc/at.deny.exists: False /etc/at.deny.group_gid: /etc/at.deny.mode: /etc/at.deny.mode_int: /etc/at.deny.others_write: /etc/at.deny.owner_uid: /etc/at.deny.path: /etc/at.deny /etc/cron.allow.exists: False /etc/cron.allow.group_gid: /etc/cron.allow.mode: /etc/cron.allow.mode_int: /etc/cron.allow.others_write: /etc/cron.allow.owner_uid: /etc/cron.allow.path: /etc/cron.allow /etc/cron.deny.exists: True /etc/cron.deny.group_gid: 0 /etc/cron.deny.is_dir: False /etc/cron.deny.mode: 0o644 /etc/cron.deny.mode_int: 420 /etc/cron.deny.others_execute: False /etc/cron.deny.others_write: False /etc/cron.deny.owner_uid: 0 /etc/cron.deny.path: /etc/cron.deny /usr/bin/crontab.exists: True /usr/bin/crontab.group_gid: 0 /usr/bin/crontab.is_dir: False /usr/bin/crontab.mode: 0o4755 /usr/bin/crontab.mode_int: 2541 /usr/bin/crontab.others_execute: True /usr/bin/crontab.others_write: False /usr/bin/crontab.owner_uid: 0 /usr/bin/crontab.path: /usr/bin/crontab /usr/bin/crontab: 4750, /var/spool/cron/<user>: 600, /etc/cron.allow: 640, /etc/at.allow: 640 (소유자 root) 1. Cron 작업 파일 권한 설정(others 읽기 쓰기 권한 제거) # chmod 750 /usr/bin/crontab # chmod o-rw /var/spool/cron/crontabs/<cron_filename> # chmod o-rw /var/spool/cron/<cron_filename> -rw------- 1 root root 40 Aug 1 10:00 /var/spool/cron/root 2. at 접근제어 파일 소유자 및 권한 설정(소유자 : root, 권한 640 이하) # chmod 640 <at.allow_filepath> <at.deny_filepath> -rw-r-----. 1 root root 1 Sep 29 2022 /etc/at.allow -rw-r-----. 1 root root 1 Sep 29 2022 /etc/at.deny 3. cron.allow, cron.deny 파일 소유자 및 권한 설정(소유자 : root, 권한 640 이하) # chmod 640 <cron.allow_filepath> <cron.deny_filepath> -rw-r-----. 1 root root 0 Oct 1 2022 /etc/cron.allow -rw-r-----. 1 root root 0 Oct 1 2022 /etc/cron.deny ※ 불필요한 경우 at 접근제어, cron.allow, cron.deny 파일 등이 존재하지 않아도 무방하며 필요한 cron 서비스 관련 설정 파일 생성 시 소유자 및 권한 설정 필요 ■ 참고 : crontab 명령어(cron.allow, cron.deny), at 명령어(at.allow, at.deny) 사용 제한 설정 - cron.allow, at.allow : .allow 파일에 등록된 계정만 명령어 사용 가능 - cron.deny, at.deny : .deny 파일에 등록된 계정만 명령어 사용 불가능 - .allow 파일만 있는 경우 : .allow 파일에 등록된 계정만 명령어 사용 가능 - .deny 파일만 있는 경우 : .deny 파일에 등록된 계정을 제외한 모든 계정이 명령어 사용 가능 - .allow, .deny 파일 둘 다 없는 경우 : SuperUser(root 계정)만 명령어 사용 가능 - .allow, .deny 파일에 같은 계정이 있는 경우 : 해당 계정만 명령어 사용 가능 cron_permission_mismatch /etc/at.allow: exists: False group_gid: mode: mode_int: others_write: owner_uid: path: /etc/at.allow
/etc/at.deny: exists: False group_gid: mode: mode_int: others_write: owner_uid: path: /etc/at.deny
/etc/cron.allow: exists: False group_gid: mode: mode_int: others_write: owner_uid: path: /etc/cron.allow
/etc/cron.deny: exists: True group_gid: 0 is_dir: False mode: 0o644 mode_int: 420 others_execute: False others_write: False owner_uid: 0 path: /etc/cron.deny
/usr/bin/crontab: exists: True group_gid: 0 is_dir: False mode: 0o4755 mode_int: 2541 others_execute: True others_write: False owner_uid: 0 path: /usr/bin/crontab

FP-023 파일권한 불필요하게 SUID, SGID bit가 설정된 파일 제거 ERROR RHEL 8 기본 SUID/SGID 목록과 비교 후 추가된 파일은 사유 검토. 불필요 시 chmod -s 1. 불필요한 SUID, SGID 설정 제거 # chmod -s <file_name> ※ "-s" : "setuid", "setgid" 설정 모두 제거하는 옵션 ※ SUID, SGID bit 제거 시 OS 및 응용 프로그램 등 서비스 정상 작동 유무 확인 필요 2. 업무상 필요한 경우 특정 그룹에서만 사용 가능하도록 그룹 제한 후 SUID 설정 # chgrp <group_name> <file_name> # chmod 4750 <file_name> -rwsr-x---. 1 user_name group_name 0 Sep 1 18:00 file_name ※ 예시 설정 : 설정한 "group_name" 그룹 내 사용자만 "file_name" 파일의 파일 소유자 권한으로 파일 실행하도록 제한 ■ 참고 : 일반적으로 불필요한 SUID/SGID 목록 [Linux] /sbin/dump : 파일 시스템 Backup 명령어 /sbin/restore : 파일 시스템 Restore 명령어 /sbin/unix_chkpwd : 사용자의 암호가 읽을 수 없는 장소에 보관되는 경우 사용자의 암호를 검사해주는 프로그램. 이 프로그램을 호출한 사용자의 암호를 검사해주는 역할만 함 /usr/bin/at : 지정된 시간에 실행할 작업을 입력하고, 대기 목록을 확인하고, 제거하는 명령어 /usr/bin/lpq : 라인프린터 작업 큐 조회 명령어 /usr/bin/lpq-lpd : (Daemons) /usr/bin/lpr : 콘솔환경에서 명시된 파일을 인쇄할 때 사용 /usr/bin/lpr-lpd : (Daemons) /usr/bin/lprm : lpq 명령어로 볼 수 있는 작업 큐를 살펴보고 해당하는 작업을 취소하거나 작업 번호를 지정하여 작업 번호에 해당하는 큐를 삭제 /usr/bin/lprm-lpd : (Daemons) /usr/bin/newgrp : 현재 세션의 사용자 그룹 변경(지정한 그룹의 쉘로 환경이 바로 변경) /usr/sbin/lpc : 커맨드 기반의 프린터 제어 /usr/sbin/lpc-lpd : (Daemons) /usr/sbin/traceroute : 네트워크 경로 출력 명령어 /usr/dt/bin/dtaction : 지정된 인수로 CDE 작업을 호출 /usr/sbin/mount : 파일시스템을 지정된 위치에서 사용 가능하도록 연결 /usr/dt/bin/dtterm : 데스크탑 기본 터미널 에뮬레이터 /usr/sbin/lchangelv : 논리적 볼륨과 연관되는 명령어 /usr/bin/X11/xlock : X 터미널을 잠그기 위한 프로그램 /opt/perf/bin/glance : 성능 모니터링 툴(CUI) /opt/perf/bin/gpm : 성능 모니터링 툴(GUI) /opt/video/lbin/camServer /usr/bin/at : (Daemons) 지정된 시간에 실행할 작 evaluator_exception

pam_tally --user <username> # pam_tally2 --user <username> # faillock --user <username> <예시> pam_faillock.so, pam_tally2.so 라이브러리 설치된 경우 # faillock --user test // pam_faillock.so 사용 test: When Type Source Valid 2023-08-01 10:00:00 RHOST localhost V 2023-08-01 10:00:05 RHOST localhost V 2023-08-01 10:00:10 RHOST localhost V # SV-003 서비스 DNS Recursive Query 제한 설정 여부 FAIL active_state: inactive enabled_state: 외부 DNS: recursion no; / 내부 캐시 DNS: recursion yes; allow-recursion { <내부망>; }; 1. DNS Recursive Query 제한 설정: "recursion no" 설정 ≪ BIND 8 ≫ [Linux, AIX, HP-UX, SunOS] # vi /etc/named.conf # vi /etc/bind/named.conf # vi /etc/bind/named.conf.options options{ recursion no; ... }; ≪ BIND 9 이상 ≫ [Linux, AIX, HP-UX, SunOS] # vi /etc/named.conf # vi /etc/bind/named.conf # vi /etc/bind/named.conf.options options{ recursion no; ... }; ※ "named.conf" 에 "named.conf.options" 를 include 하는 구문이 있으면 해당 파일에 설정 권장 2. DNS 서비스 재시작 ■ 참고 : DNS Recursive Query 를 사용하는 경우 ACL 또는 "allow-recursion" 구문으로 호스트 제한 설정 ≪ BIND 8 ≫ : "allow-recursion { "none"; };" 또는 "allow-recursion" 구문 내 호스트 제한 설정 [Linux, AIX, HP-UX, SunOS] # vi /etc/named.conf # vi /etc/bind/named.conf # vi /etc/bind/named.conf.options options{ recursion yes; allow-recursion { "none"; }; ... }; 또는 options{ recursion yes; allow-recursion { <ip_address>; }; ... }; ≪ BIND 9 이상 ≫ : "allow-recursion { "none"; };" 또는 ACL 설정, "allow-recursion" 구문 내 호스트 제한 설정 [Linux, AIX, HP-UX, SunOS] # vi /etc/named.conf # vi /etc/bind/named.conf # vi /etc/bind/named.conf.options options{ recursion yes; allow-recursion { "none"; }; ... }; 또는 options{ acl trust { 192.168.1.0/24; }; allow-recursion { trust; }; ... }; 또는 options{ allow-recursion { <ip_address>; }; ... }; service_enabled :
: inactive

SV-020 서비스 불필요한 SMTP 서비스 비활성화 FAIL active_state: inactive enabled_state: inet_interfaces: 외부 메일 송신 불필요 시: postfix disabled / 로컬 알림 필요 시: inet_interfaces=127.0.0.1 1. 업무상 불필요한 SMTP 서비스 중지 및 서비스 재시작 설정 해제 ≪ sendmail ≫ [Linux] # service sendmail stop # chkconfig sendmail off 또는 # systemctl stop sendmail.service # systemctl disable sendmail.service [AIX 7.2, 7.3] # stopsrc -s sendmail # chrctcp -d sendmail [AIX 7.1 이하] : sendmail 서비스 중지 및 rc.tcpip 스크립트 설정 주석 처리 # stopsrc -s sendmail # vi /etc/rc.tcpip #start /usr/lib/sendmail "$src_running" "-bd -q${qpi}" # /sbin/init.d/sendmail stop # vi /etc/rc.config.d/mailservs SENDMAIL_SERVER=0 [SunOS 5.10, 5.11] # svcadm disable svc:/network/sendmail-client # svcadm disable svc:/network/smtp:sendmail [SunOS 5.9 이하] # /etc/init.d/sendmail stop # ls -al /etc/rc*.d/* | grep sendmail # ls -al /etc/rc.d/rc*.d/* | grep sendmail # mv /etc/rc<run_level>.d/S<service_number>sendmail /etc/rc<run_level>.d/S<service_nember>sendmail.orig ≪ postfix ≫ [Linux] # service postfix stop # chkconfig postfix off 또는 # systemctl stop postfix.service # systemctl disable postfix.service [AIX 7.2, 7.3] # stopsrc -s postfix # chrctcp -d postfix [AIX 7.1] : postfix 서비스 중지 및 rc.tcpip 스크립트 설정 주석 처리 # stopsrc -s postfix # vi /etc/rc.tcpip [SunOS 5.10, 5.11] # svcadm disable <postfix_service> [SunOS 5.9 이하] # kill -9 <PID> # ls -al /etc/rc*.d/* | grep postfix # ls -al /etc/rc.d/rc*.d/* | grep postfix # mv /etc/rc<run_level>.d/S<service_number>postfix /etc/rc<run_level>.d/S<service_number>postfix.orig ≪ exim ≫ [Linux] # service exim stop # c service_enabled :
: inactive
SV-024 서비스 SMTP 서비스의 DoS 방지 기능 설정 여부 FAIL default_process_limit: message_size_limit: smtpd_client_connection_count_limit: smtpd_recipient_limit: postfix: message_size_limit=10240000(10MB), default_process_limit=100, smtpd_recipient_limit=100, smtpd_client_connection_count_limit=20 1. SMTP 서비스 설정 파일 DoS 방지 기능 설정 ≪ sendmail ≫ # vi /etc/sendmail.cf # vi /etc/mail/sendmail.cf O MinFreeBlocks=100 O MaxMessageSize=1000000 O MaxDaemonChildren=12 O ConnectionRateThrottle=12 O MaxHeadersLength=32768 ※ mc 파일을 편집하는 경우 m4 macro 로 cf 파일 생성하여 설정 적용 # m4 sendmail.mc > sendmail.cf ≪ postfix ≫ # vi /etc/postfix/main.cf message_size_limit header_size_limit default_process_limit local_destination_concurrency_limit smtpd_recipient_limit ≪ exim ≫ # vi /etc/exim.conf # vi /etc/exim/exim.conf # vi /etc/exim/exim4.conf # vi /etc/exim4/conf.d/*.conf message_size_limit header_maxsize queue_run_max recipients_max 2. SMTP 서비스 재시작 ※ postfix 는 "postfix reload" 명령어로 설정 변경 적용 가능 postfix_limit_missing /etc/postfix/main.cf:
SV-025 서비스 SMTP 서비스 스팸 메일 릴레이 제한 설정 여부 FAIL mynetworks: smtpd_relay_restrictions: postfix: smtpd_relay_restrictions = permit_mynetworks, reject_unauth_destination. mynetworks = 127.0.0.0/8, <내부망> 1. (8.9 버전 미만) 스팸 메일 릴레이 제한 설정 # vi /etc/sendmail.cf # vi /etc/mail/sendmail.cf R$* $#error $@ 5.7.1 $: "550 Relaying denied" ※ mc 파일을 편집하는 경우 m4 macro 로 cf 파일 생성하여 설정 적용 # m4 sendmail.mc > sendmail.cf 1-3. /etc/mail/access 에 네트워크 접근 제한 설정 후 /etc/mail/access.db 에 설정 적용(/etc/mail/access 파일이 없으면 파일 생성하여 설정) # vi /etc/mail/access Connect:localhost.localdomain RELAY Connect:localhost RELAY Connect:127.0.0.1 RELAY Connect:<sevice_domain> REJECT (Access DB 를 사용하는 경우) # makemap dbm /etc/mail/access.db < /etc/mail/access (Berkeley DB 를 사용하는 경우) # makemap hash /etc/mail/access.db < /etc/mail/access ≪ postfix ≫ : (smtpd_relay_restrictions=permit_mynetworks,reject 인 경우) 과도하게 설정된 허용 네트워크 값 제거 # vi /etc/postfix/main.cf mynetworks = 192.168.217.1/24, 127.0.0.1/8 ≪ exim ≫ : (acl_smtp_rcpt 에 설정되어 있는 ACL 설정에서) 과도하게 설정되어 있거나 불필요한 호스트 설정 제거 # vi /etc/exim.conf # vi /etc/exim/exim.conf # vi /etc/exim/exim4.conf # vi /etc/exim4/conf.d/*.conf (수정 전) accept hosts = 0.0.0.0 : 192.168.217.1 : *.example.com (수정 후) accept hosts = 192.168.217.1 ※ SMTP 서버 운영 환경에 맞게 스팸 메일 릴레이 제한 추가 설정 진행 필요시 아래 URL 참고 : https://spam.kisa.or.kr/spam/cm/cntnts/cntntsView.do?mi=1085&cntn relay_restriction_unsafe /etc/postfix/main.cf:

SV-046 서비스 원격 터미널 접속 타임아웃 설정 여부 FAIL ClientAliveCountMax: ClientAliveInterval: TMOUT: TMOUT=600 (10분) 또는 sshd_config: ClientAliveInterval 300, ClientAliveCountMax 2 (10분) ClientAliveCountMax)' /etc/ssh/sshd_config 결과 ClientAliveInterval × CountMax = 900초(15분) 이하이면 정상으로 판단한다. | [Linux, AIX, HP-UX, SunOS] 1. Telnet 서비스 Session Timeout 설정 ≪ sh, ksh, bash ≫ # vi /etc/profile # vi /etc/.profile TMOUT=900 export TMOUT ≪ csh ≫ # vi /etc/csh.login # vi /etc/csh.cshrc set autologout=15 2. SSH 서비스 Session Timeout 설정 # vi /etc/sshd_config # vi /etc/ssh/sshd_config # vi /opt/ssh/etc/sshd_config # vi /usr/local/etc/sshd_config # vi /usr/local/sshd/etc/sshd_config # vi /usr/local/ssh/etc/sshd_config ClientAliveInterval 5m # 5 minutes ClientAliveCountMax 3 # 3 times ※ "ClientAliveInterval 5m, ClientAliveCountMax 3" 설정 시 15분(5분 X 3회) 후 SSH 서비스 세션 종료 ※ "ClientAliveInterval 60, ClientAliveCountMax 15" 설정 시 15분(60초 X 15회) 후 SSH 서비스 세션 종료 3. SSH 서비스 재시작 1. Session Timeout 설정 # vi /etc/default/login TIMEOUT=900 timeout_policy_missing /etc/profile: # /etc/profile # System wide environment and startup programs, for login setup # Functions and aliases go in /etc/bashrc # It's NOT a good idea to change this file unless you know what you # are doing. It's much better to create a custom.sh shell script in # /etc/profile.d/ to make custom changes to your environment, as this # will prevent the need for merging in future updates. pathmunge () { case ":${PATH}:" in *:"$1":*) ;; *) if [ "$2" = "after" ] ; then PATH=$PATH:$1 else PATH=$1:$PATH fi esac } if [ -x /usr/bin/id ]; then if [ -z "$EUID" ]; then # ksh workaround EUID=`/usr/bin/id -u` UID=`/usr/bin/id -ru` fi USER="`/usr/bin/id -un`" LOGNAME=$USER MAIL="/var/spool/mail/$USER" fi # Path manipulation if [ "$EUID" = "0" ]; then pathmunge /usr/sbin pathmunge /usr/local/sbin else pathmunge /usr/local/sbin after pathmunge /usr/sbin after fi HOSTNAME=`/usr/bin/hostname 2>/dev/null` HISTSIZE=1000 if [ "$HISTCONTROL" = "ignorespace" ] ; then export HISTCONTROL=ignoreboth else export HISTCONTROL=ignoredups fi export PATH USER LOGNAME MAIL HOSTNAME HISTSIZE HISTCONTROL # By default, we want umask to get set. This sets it for login shell # Current threshold for system reserved uid/gids is 200 # You could check uidgid reservation validity in # /usr/share/doc/setup-*/uidgid file if [ $UID -gt 199 ] && [ "`/usr/bin/id -gn`" = "`/usr/bin/id -un`" ]; then umask 002 else umask 022 fi for i in /etc/profile.d/*.sh /etc/profile.d/sh.local ; do if [ -r "$i" ]; then if [ "${-#*i}" != "$-" ]; then . "$i" else . "$i" >/dev/null fi fi done unset i unset -f pathmunge if [ -n "${BASH_VERSION-}" ] ; then if [ -f /etc/bashrc ] ; then # Bash login shells run only /etc/profile # Bash non-login shells run only /etc/bashrc # Check for double sourcing is done in /etc/bashrc. . /etc/bashrc fi fi
/etc/ssh/sshd_config: # $OpenBSD: sshd_config,v 1.103 2018/04/09 20:41:22 tj Exp $ # This is the sshd server system-wide configuration file. SY-004 시스템 kdump 구성 상태 FAIL active_state: active core_collector: makedumpfile -l --message-level 7 -d 31 crashkernel: auto enabled: True kdump active(running) + enabled, crashkernel=auto(또는 메모리>4GB 시 1G-:512M,4G-:768M,64G-:2G 형태), core_collector=makedumpfile -l --message-level 1 -d 31 * kdump 미기동 시 # systemctl enable kdump # systemctl start kdump # systemctl status kdump (loaded/active 확인) # crashkernel 설정 필요 시 # vi /etc/default/grub → crashkernel=auto 추가 # grub2-mkconfig -o /boot/grub2/grub.cfg core_collector_mismatch systemctl is-active kdump: active
/etc/default/grub: GRUB_CMDLINE_LINUX="console=tty0 console=ttyS0,115200n8 net.ifnames=0 rd.blacklist=nouveau nvme_core.io_timeout=4294967295 crashkernel=auto" GRUB_TIMEOUT=0 GRUB_ENABLE_BLSCFG=true GRUB_DEFAULT=saved
/etc/kdump.conf: # This file contains a series of commands to perform (in order) in the kdump # kernel after a kernel crash in the crash kernel(1st kernel) has happened. # # Directives in this file are only applicable to the kdump initramfs, and have # no effect once the root filesystem is mounted and the normal init scripts are # processed. # # Currently, only one dump target and path can be specified. If the dumping to # the configured target fails, the failure action which can be configured via # the "failure_action" directive will be performed. # # Supported options: # # raw <partition> # - Will dd /proc/vmcore into <partition>. # Use persistent device names for partition devices, # such as /dev/vg/<devname>. # # nfs <nfs mount> # - Will mount nfs to <mnt>, and copy /proc/vmcore to # <mnt>/<path>/%HOST-%DATE/, supports DNS. # # ssh <user@server> # - Will save /proc/vmcore to <user@server>:<path>/%HOST-%DATE/, # supports DNS. # NOTE: make sure the user has write permissions on the server. # # sshkey <path> # - Will use the sshkey to do ssh dump. # Specify the path of the ssh key to use when dumping # via ssh. The default value is /root/.ssh/kdump_id_rsa. # # <fs type> <partition> # - Will mount -t <fs type> <partition> <mnt>, and copy # /proc/vmcore to <mnt>/<path>/%DATE/. # NOTE: <partition> can be a device node, label or uuid. # It's recommended to use persistent device names # such as /dev/vg/<devname>. # Otherwise it's suggested to use label or uuid. # # path <path> # - "path" represents the file system path in which vmcore # will be saved. If a dump target is specified in # kdump.conf, then "path" is relative to the specified # dump target. # # Interpretation of "path" changes a bit if the user didn't # specify any dump target explicitly in kdump.conf. In this # case, "path" represents the absolute path from root. The # dump target and adjusted path are arrived at automatically # depending on what's mounted in the current system. # # Ignored for raw device dumps. If unset, will use the default # "/var/crash". # # core_collector <command> <options> # - This allows you to specify the command to copy # the vmcore. The default is makedumpfile, which on # some architectures can drastically reduce vmcore size. # See /sbin/makedumpfile --help for a list of options. # Note that the -i and -g options are not needed here, # as the initrd will automatically be populated with a # config file appropriate for the running kernel. # The default core_collector for raw/ssh dump is: # "makedumpfile -F -l --message-level 7 -d 31". # The default core_collector for other targets is: # "makedumpfile -l --message-level 7 -d 31". # # "makedumpfile -F" will create a flattened vmcore. # You need to use "makedumpfile -R" to rearrange the dump data to # a normal dumpfile readable with analysis tools. For example: # "makedumpfile -R vmcore < vmcore.flat". # # For core_collector format details, you can refer to # kexec-kdump-howto.txt or kdump.conf manpage. # # kdump_post <binary | script> # - This directive allows you to run a executable binary # or script after the vmcore dump process terminates. # The exit status of the current dump process is fed to # the executable binary or script as its first argument. # All files under /etc/kdump/post.d are collectively sorted # and executed in lexical order, before binary or script # specified kdump_post parameter is executed. # # kdump_pre <binary | script> # - Works like the "kdump_post" directive, but instead of running # after the dump process, runs immediately before it. # Exit status of this binary is interpreted as follows: # 0 - continue with dump process as usual # non 0 - run the final action (reboot/poweroff/halt) # All files under /etc/kdump/pre.d are collectively sorted and # executed in lexical order, after binary or script specified # kdump_pre parameter is executed. # Even if the binary or script in /etc/kdump/pre.d directory # returns non 0 exit status, the processing is continued. # # extra_bins <binaries | shell scripts> # - This directive allows you to specify additional binaries or # shell scripts to be included in the kdump initrd. # Generally they are useful in conjunction with a kdump_post # or kdump_pre binary or script which depends on these extra_bins. # # extra_modules <module(s)> # - This directive allows you to specify extra kernel modules # that you want to be loaded in the kdump initrd. # Multiple modules can be listed, separated by spaces, and any # dependent modules will automatically be included. # # failure_action <reboot | halt | poweroff | shell | dump_to_rootfs> # - Action to perform in case dumping fails. # reboot: Reboot the system. # halt: Halt the system. # poweroff: Power down the system. # shell: Drop to a bash shell. # Exiting the shell reboots the system by default, # or perform "final_action". # dump_to_rootfs: Dump vmcore to rootfs from initramfs context and # reboot by default or perform "final_action". # Useful when non-root dump target is specified. # The default option is "reboot". # # default <reboot | halt | poweroff | shell | dump_to_rootfs> # - Same as the "failure_action" directive above, but this directive # is obsolete and will be removed in the future. # # final_action <reboot | halt | poweroff> # - Action to perform in case dumping succeeds. Also performed # when "shell" or "dump_to_rootfs" failure action finishes. # Each action is same as the "failure_action" directive above. # The default is "reboot". # # force_rebuild <0 | 1> # - By default, kdump initrd will only be rebuilt when necessary. # Specify 1 to force rebuilding kdump initrd every time when kdump # service starts. # # force_no_rebuild <0 | 1> # - By default, kdump initrd will be rebuilt when necessary. # Specify 1 to bypass rebuilding of kdump initrd. # # force_no_rebuild and force_rebuild options are mutually # exclusive and they should not be set to 1 simultaneously. # # override_resettable <0 | 1> # - Usually an unresettable block device can't be a dump target. # Specifying 1 when you want to dump even though the block # target is unresettable # By default, it is 0, which will not try dumping destined to fail. # # dracut_args <arg(s)> # - Pass extra dracut options when rebuilding kdump initrd. # # fence_kdump_args <arg(s)> # - Command line arguments for fence_kdump_send (it can contain # all valid arguments except hosts to send notification to). # # fence_kdump_nodes <node(s)> # - List of cluster node(s) except localhost, separated by spaces, # to send fence_kdump notifications to. # (this option is mandatory to enable fence_kdump). # #raw /dev/vg/lv_kdump #ext4 /dev/vg/lv_kdump #ext4 LABEL=/boot #ext4 UUID=03138356-5e61-4ab3-b58e-27507ac41937 #nfs my.server.com:/export/tmp #nfs [2001:db8::1:2:3:4]:/export/tmp #ssh user@my.server.com #ssh user@2001:db8::1:2:3:4 #sshkey /root/.ssh/kdump_id_rsa path /var/crash core_collector makedumpfile -l --message-level 7 -d 31 #core_collector scp #kdump_post /var/crash/scripts/kdump-post.sh #kdump_pre /var/crash/scripts/kdump-pre.sh #extra_bins /usr/bin/lftp #extra_modules gfs2 #failure_action shell #force_rebuild 1 #force_no_rebuild 1 #dracut_args --omit-drivers "cfg80211 snd" --add-drivers "ext2 ext3" #fence_kdump_args -p 7410 -f auto -c 0 -i 10 #fence_kdump_nodes node1 node2
/etc/systemd/system/multi-user.target.wants/kdump.service: present
/proc/cmdline: BOOT_IMAGE=(hd0,gpt3)/boot/vmlinuz-4.18.0-553.54.1.el8_10.x86_64 root=UUID=0988a781-7c57-45f4-96aa-ec53adc36546 console=tty0 console=ttyS0,115200n8 net.ifnames=0 rd.blacklist=nouveau nvme_core.io_timeout=4294967295 crashkernel=auto

/etc/rsyslog.conf: # rsyslog configuration file # For more information see /usr/share/doc/rsyslog-*/rsyslog_conf.html # or latest version online at http://www.rsyslog.com/doc/rsyslog_conf.html # If you experience problems, see http://www.rsyslog.com/doc/troubleshoot.html #### MODULES #### module(load="imuxsock" # provides support for local system logging (e.g. via logger command) SysSock.Use="off") # Turn off message reception via local log socket; # local messages are retrieved through imjournal now. module(load="imjournal" # provides access to the systemd journal UsePid="system" # PID nummber is retrieved as the ID of the process the journal entry originates from StateFile="imjournal.state") # File to store the position in the journal #module(load="imklog") # reads kernel messages (the same are read from journald) #module(load="immark") # provides --MARK-- message capability # Provides UDP syslog reception # for parameters see http://www.rsyslog.com/doc/imudp.html #module(load="imudp") # needs to be done just once #input(type="imudp" port="514") # Provides TCP syslog reception # for parameters see http://www.rsyslog.com/doc/imtcp.html #module(load="imtcp") # needs to be done just once #input(type="imtcp" port="514") #### GLOBAL DIRECTIVES #### # Where to place auxiliary files global(workDirectory="/var/lib/rsyslog") # Use default timestamp format module(load="builtin:omfile" Template="RSYSLOG_TraditionalFileFormat") # Include all config files in /etc/rsyslog.d/ include(file="/etc/rsyslog.d/*.conf" mode="optional") #### RULES #### # Log all kernel messages to the console. # Logging much else clutters up the screen. #kern.* /dev/console # Log anything (except mail) of level info or higher. # Don't log private authentication messages! *.info;mail.none;authpriv.none;cron.none /var/log/messages # The authpriv file has restricted access. authpriv.* /var/log/secure # Log all the mail messages in one place. mail.* -/var/log/maillog # Log cron stuff cron.* /var/log/cron # Everybody gets emergency messages *.emerg :omusrmsg:* # Save news errors of level crit and higher in a special file. uucp,news.crit /var/log/spooler # Save boot messages also to boot.log local7.* /var/log/boot.log # ### sample forwarding rule ### #action(type="omfwd" # An on-disk queue is created for this action. If the remote host is # down, messages are spooled to disk and sent when it is up again. #queue.filename="fwdRule1" # unique name prefix for spool files #queue.maxdiskspace="1g" # 1gb space limit (use as much as possible) #queue.saveonshutdown="on" # save messages to disk on shutdown #queue.type="LinkedList" # run asynchronously #action.resumeRetryCount="-1" # infinite retries if host is down # Remote Logging (we use TCP for reliable delivery) # remote_host is: name/ip, e.g. 192.168.0.1, port optional e.g. 10514 #Target="remote_host" Port="XXX" Protocol="tcp")

/etc/sysconfig/irqbalance: # irqbalance is a daemon process that distributes interrupts across # CPUS on SMP systems. The default is to rebalance once every 10 # seconds. This is the environment file that is specified to systemd via the # EnvironmentFile key in the service unit file (or via whatever method the init # system you're using has. # # ONESHOT=yes # after starting, wait for a minute, then look at the interrupt # load and balance it once; after balancing exit and do not change # it again. #IRQBALANCE_ONESHOT= # # IRQBALANCE_BANNED_CPUS # 64 bit bitmask which allows you to indicate which cpu's should # be skipped when reblancing irqs. Cpu numbers which have their # corresponding bits set to one in this mask will not have any # irq's assigned to them on rebalance # #IRQBALANCE_BANNED_CPUS= # # IRQBALANCE_ARGS # append any args here to the irqbalance daemon as documented in the man page # #IRQBALANCE_ARGS=
SY-029 시스템 내장 디스크 볼륨 그룹 명명 규칙 준수 확인 WARN 내장 디스크 VG 명명: int_vg{NN} 형식 100% 준수. 외장은 별도 규칙({hostname8}_vg{NN}) vgs --noheadings -o vg_name 2>/dev/null | awk '{print $1}' | while read VG; do echo "VG: $VG" echo " [1-3] 디스크구분: ${VG:0:3} (기준: int)" echo " [4] 구분자: ${VG:3:1} (기준: _)" echo " [5-6] 볼륨명: ${VG:4:2} (기준: vg)" echo " [7-8] 일련번호: ${VG:6:2} (기준: 01~99)" if echo "$VG" | grep -Pq '^int_vg[0-9]{2}$'; then echo " 판정: PASS" else echo " 판정: FAIL" fi echo "---" done partial_collection vgs:
SY-030 시스템 Logical 볼륨 명명 규칙 준수 확인 WARN LV 명명: lv_{용도명} 형식. 동일 용도 복수 시 끝에 숫자 순번 lvs --noheadings -o lv_name,vg_name 2>/dev/null | awk '{print $1, $2}' | while read LV VG; do echo "LV: $LV (VG: $VG)" echo " [1-2] 접두사: ${LV:0:2} (기준: lv)" echo " [3] 구분자: ${LV:2:1} (기준: _)" echo " [4-] 용도명: ${LV:3}" if echo "$LV" | grep -Pq '^lv_[a-z][a-z0-9]*[0-9]?$'; then echo " 판정: PASS" else echo " 판정: FAIL" fi echo "---" done partial_collection lvs:
SY-031 시스템 tuned-profile 구성 동기화 WARN active_profile: virtual-guest 동일 클러스터 노드 간 동일 tuned-profile (보통 throughput-performance) # tuned-adm profile throughput-performance (또는 latency-performance, 워크로드에 맞게 선택) # tuned-adm active (확인) ※ 동일 클러스터 내 모든 노드 동일 적용 partial_collection tuned-adm active: Current active profile: virtual-guest
